< review>
How disappointing. I have tried on a couple occasions to give this place a chance, but after the last time and having the exact same experience I am done going. This place could be so cool if it had staff that actually cared. My husband and I took our 2 year old and newborn last time. It cost $20 to get in. There was 3 girla working at the front desk. Or one working and 2 talking, not sure but that is how it appeared especially when every station was a complete disaster and no one to be found helping. The art areas were a mess, you couldn't tell what was to be used, thrown away, if the items were a child's that they left to get later. Upstairs the children and parents were getting frustrated and short with eachother because no one could agree on how the ball machines and ball drop worked. It was A MESS ! So much unnecessary confusion and frustration. All the place needs is an employee to care! Someone needs to be upstairs to help guests with questions and keeping the place tidy. We ended up just leaving and going to the park. Very disappointing. .. again.<//review>

< Review>
Good place to make your own copies and print documents. You can email your documents to "printandgo@fedex.com" then print them at the store with a code sent to your email. You get a card at the store and add cash to it or use your credit card. PAY ATTENTION OR YOU LOSE MONEY: the copy machines are set to COLOR Copies! You must change your choice to BLACK & WHITE! If you don't, you pay for color, which is expensive. Not sure why the default choice is color. I would give 5 stars on the copying if this was corrected.<//Review>

< Review>
*** (Hawthorne) ***
Made a quick stop to send off some goods. This Fedex is located in a super busy part of town right off of the 405 freeway Hawthorne exit.

Here's what liked...
* The location is convenient being right off of the freeway. However accessing the lot can be difficult.
* Love the customer service. The ladies at the front register were super friendly and helpful! I was caught off guard by the genuine smile and quick service :-)
* The parking lot for 8:30 am was excellent.
* There are plenty of places to eat in the plaza if you need a one-stop-shop location.

Here's what I didn't like...
* Accessing plaza was difficult with the rush hour traffic.</Review>
